	<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of geological features on Venus</h1>
	
	<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
		<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>This is a <b>list of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Geological_features" title="Geological features">geological features</a> on <a href="/wiki/Venus" title="Venus">Venus</a></b>. Venus is the second planet from the Sun. Venus is classified as a <a href="/wiki/Terrestrial_planet" title="Terrestrial planet">terrestrial planet</a> and it is sometimes called Earth's "sister planet" owing to their similar size, gravity, and bulk composition (Venus is both the closest planet to Earth and the planet closest in size to Earth). The surface of Venus is covered by a dense atmosphere and presents clear evidence of former violent volcanic activity. It has shield and composite volcanoes similar to those found on Earth.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Valles">Valles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_geological_features_on_Venus&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Valles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Cytherean" title="Cytherean">Cytherean</a> valleys are called by the Latin term <i>valles</i>, and are named after river goddesses or after words for 'Venus' in other languages.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Undae">Undae</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_geological_features_on_Venus&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Undae">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Undae" title="Undae">Undae</a> on Venus refer to <a href="/wiki/Dune" title="Dune">dune</a> fields and are named after desert goddesses.
</p>

<th>Name</th>

<th>Name origin
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Al-Uzza_Undae&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Al-Uzza Undae (page does not exist)">Al-Uzza Undae</a></td>
<td>67.7N</td>
<td>90.5E</td>
<td>150</td>
<td>1994</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Al-%E2%80%98Uzz%C3%A1" title="Al-‘Uzzá">Al-‘Uzzá</a>, Arabian desert goddess.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Menat_Undae&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Menat Undae (page does not exist)">Menat Undae</a></td>
<td>24.8S</td>
<td>339.4E</td>
<td>100</td>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tesserae">Tesserae</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_geological_features_on_Venus&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Tesserae">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tessera_(Venusian_geography)" title="Tessera (Venusian geography)">Tesserae</a> are areas of <a href="/wiki/Polygon" title="Polygon">polygonal</a> terrain. They are named after goddesses in world mythologies.
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th>Name</th>
<th>Latitude</th>
<th>Longitude</th>
<th>Diameter (km)</th>
<th>Year named</th>
<th>Name origin
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Adrasthea_Tesserae" title="Adrasthea Tesserae">Adrasthea Tesserae</a></td>
<td>30.0N</td>
<td>55.0E</td>
<td>750.0</td>
<td>1997</td>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Adrasteia_(goddess)" title="Adrasteia (goddess)">Adrastea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Greece" title="Ancient Greece">Greek</a> goddess of <a href="/wiki/Law" title="Law">law</a>.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rupes">Rupes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_geological_features_on_Venus&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Rupes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
